+// Helper to reliably get month names in pt-BR
+function monthName(offsetMonths = 0) {
+    const d = new Date()
+    d.setMonth(d.getMonth() - offsetMonths)
+    // Usando formatação manual para evitar bugs de locale em server components
+    const months = [
+        "Janeiro", "Fevereiro", "Março", "Abril", "Maio", "Junho",
+        "Julho", "Agosto", "Setembro", "Outubro", "Novembro", "Dezembro"
+    ]
+    return months[d.getMonth()]

 function isUuid(v: string) {
     return /^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{12}$/i.test(v.trim())
 }
 
 function sanitizeForOrIlike(v: string) {
     // PostgREST `or()` uses comma-separated expressions, so avoid commas/parentheses/wildcards.
     return v.replace(/[,%()]/g, " ").trim()
 }

+function buildPropertiesPageHref(
+    page: number,
+    pageSize: number,
+    params: Record<string, string | number | null | undefined>
+) {
+    const sp = new URLSearchParams()
+    sp.set('page', String(page))
+    sp.set('pageSize', String(pageSize))
+
+    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(params)) {
+        if (value == null) continue
+        const normalized = String(value)
+        if (!normalized || normalized === 'all') continue
+        sp.set(key, normalized)
+    }
+
+    return `/properties?${sp.toString()}`
 }

+function publicTypeLabel(type: string | null | undefined) {
+  switch (type) {
+    case "apartment":
+      return "Apartamento"
+    case "house":
+      return "Casa"
+    case "condominium_house":
+      return "Casa em condomínio"
+    case "land":
+      return "Terreno"
+    case "commercial":
+      return "Imóvel comercial"
+    case "commercial_space":
+      return "Salão comercial"
+    default:
+      return "Imóvel"
+  }
+}
+
+function publicTransactionLabel(transactionType: string | null | undefined) {
+  switch (transactionType) {
+    case "rent":
+      return "Locação"
+    case "seasonal":
+      return "Temporada"
+    case "sale":
+    default:
+      return "Venda"
+  }
+}
+
+function publicPurposeLabel(purpose: string | null | undefined) {
+  switch (purpose) {
+    case "commercial":
+      return "Comercial"
+    case "residential":
+    default:
+      return "Residencial"
+  }

+        async function fetchOwners() {
+            if (!organizationId) return
+            const { data } = await supabase
+                .from('contacts')
+                .select('id, name')
+                .eq('organization_id', organizationId)
+                .order('name')
+            if (data) setOwners(data)
+        }
+        fetchOwners()
+    }, [organizationId, supabase])
+
+    async function handleCreateOwner(e: React.FormEvent) {
+        e.preventDefault()
+        if (!newOwnerName.trim() || !organizationId) return
+        setIsCreatingOwner(true)
+        try {
+            const { data, error } = await supabase.from('contacts').insert({
+                organization_id: organizationId,
+                name: newOwnerName.trim(),
+                phone: newOwnerPhone.trim() || null,
+                type: 'owner',
+                status: 'new',
+            }).select('id, name').single()
+
+            if (error) throw error
+            if (data) {
+                setOwners(prev => [...prev, data].sort((a, b) => a.name.localeCompare(b.name)))
+                form.setValue("owner_contact_id", data.id, { shouldDirty: true })
+                form.setValue("owner_name", data.name, { shouldDirty: true })
+                setIsOwnerModalOpen(false)
+                setNewOwnerName("")
+                setNewOwnerPhone("")
+                toast.success("Proprietário criado com sucesso!")
+            }
+        } catch (error) {
+            console.error("Error creating owner:", error)
+            toast.error("Erro ao criar proprietário")
+        } finally {
+            setIsCreatingOwner(false)
+        }
+    }

+function appendThemePreviewParam(href: string, theme: SiteTheme) {
+  const [withoutHash, hashPart] = href.split("#", 2)
+  const [basePath, existingQuery] = withoutHash.split("?", 2)
+  const params = new URLSearchParams(existingQuery ?? "")
+  params.set("preview_theme", theme)
+  const query = params.toString()
